(Yes/No)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire for investigating workplace environment:

**Workplace Environmental Survey**

We value our employees' opinions about their work experience, including aspects that affect job satisfaction and overall well-being in the office space. Your honest feedback will help us improve working conditions to make your time at [Company Name] more enjoyable.

Please answer these questions based on how you feel today (or most days):

1. **Comfort Level**: How comfortable do you usually find our workspace?

a) Very uncomfortable
b) Somewhat discomforting, but manageable 
c) Neutral - it's okay as is d) Comfortable e) Extremely comfy

2. What aspects of your work environment make the biggest positive impact on productivity and job satisfaction? (Select all that apply)

* Natural light/natural views
* Temperature control/ventilation system effectiveness
* Noise level/sound quality in open spaces or private offices 
* Availability/frequency of breaks/snack areas/restrooms

3. **Communication**: How easy is it to get information you need from colleagues, supervisors, and other departments?

a) Very difficult b) Somewhat challenging c) Neutral d) Easy e) Extremely effortless 

4. Are there any specific amenities or services that would enhance your work experience? (Check all applicable)

* On-site gym/fitness classes
* Wellness programs/workshops 
* Meal delivery/catering options on site  
* Flexible workspace arrangements for remote workers

5 **Collaboration**: How often do you engage in meaningful discussions, share ideas with colleagues or supervisors?

a) Rarely b) Occasionally c) Frequently d) Almost always e) Always 

6. What are the most significant distractions that hinder your focus and productivity? (Select all applicable)

* Noise from nearby areas
* Digital notifications/social media 
* Meetings/emails/texts outside of work hours  
Other [please specify]

7 **Overall Satisfaction**: How satisfied or dissatisfied do you feel with our workplace environment?

a) Very Dissatisfied b) Somewhat Displeased c) Neutral d) Slightly Pleased e) Extremely Happy

Thank your for taking the time to share these valuable insights!

**Remote Working Experience Questionnaire**

As we continue to explore ways to improve our company's approach to telecommuting, your input and feedback are invaluable. Please take the time to share your thoughts by answering these short survey-style questions.

1. **What has been most enjoyable about working remotely?**
Please describe a specific experience or aspect of remote work that you've found particularly fulfilling (e.g., increased productivity, better balance between personal/professional life).

2. What are some common challenges have faced while telecommuting?
(Please select all applicable options:)

* Difficulty staying focused and motivated
* Limited access to company resources/technology/tools
* Feeling disconnected from colleagues/team members
* Other (please specify): _______________________

3. How do you currently prioritize your work-life balance when working remotely? 
Please rate the following statements on a scale of 1-5, where:

(4) = Strongly Agree

(Scale:)

I am able to effectively separate my personal and professional life while telecommuting.
My family/friends are understanding about not being available during traditional office hours.

3.2 How often do you take breaks or engage in self-care activities (e.g., exercise, meditation)?

4. What tools/applications have been most helpful for remote work?

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire for investigating employee experiences during their first few weeks at work, specifically focusing on "On-Boarding":

**New Hire Experience: An Exploration into Our Company's On-Bording Process**

We value your feedback and would like to hear about your experience as you start this new chapter with our company. Your input will help us refine the process for future hires.

1. **What was most exciting or impressive during my first few days onboarding?**
Please share a specific moment, interaction, or insight that stood out positively.
(Open-ended text response)

2. How would rate your overall experience in getting familiar with our company's policies and procedures?
(Scale: 5 - Very Easy to Understand; 1- Not at All Clear)
3. **What was the most helpful resource (e.g., training, mentorship) you received during onboarding?**
Please specify which resources made a significant impact or difference.
(Open-ended text response)

4. How would rate your supervisor's support and guidance throughout my first few weeks?
(Scale: 5 - Extremely Supportive; 1- Not at All Supported)
5. **What aspect of the company culture surprised you most (positively/negatively)?**
Please share any observations or insights that stood out to you.
(Open-ended text response)

6. What suggestions do you have for improving our onboarding process, if anything?
(Please provide specific ideas and/or areas where we can improve)
(Optional: If no changes are needed, please let us know why!)

Thank your new hires in advance!

**Learner Feedback Questionnaire**

(Please provide specific examples of how it may influence their workflow)

6. How do the course materials and resources align with your current needs?

(Please provide specific examples of how it may be useful)

* Mostly sure about the requirements.

b) Monthly/Semiannually: I have occasional meetings to review progress.

**Employee Feedback: Enhancing Our Team's Success**

We value our employees' insights in helping us improve processes and support their growth within the organization! Your input will help shape initiatives that benefit everyone. Please take your time to answer these thought-provoking questions honestly.

1. **What drives you?**
When working on a project or task, what motivates YOU most?

a) The opportunity for creative expression
b) Meeting deadlines and achieving goals quickly 
c) Collaborating with colleagues towards common objectives

2. What do we excel at?
Which of the following aspects makes our team stand out to me:

* Communication & teamwork skills among members
* Adaptability in responding to changing priorities or unexpected challenges
* Innovative problem-solving approaches within projects 

3. **Room for growth?**
What skill, knowledge area, or training would you like us to focus on developing further?

4. How do we measure up?
In terms of employee performance and feedback:

a) We're doing a great job in recognizing individual contributions 
b) There's room for improvement regarding timely recognition
c) I'd love more specific guidance & constructive criticism

5. **What gets lost?**
When working on tasks or projects, what do you often find yourself wishing we had (more of)?

* Clearer expectations and guidelines from management/leadership
* Additional resources/support to tackle complex challenges 
* More opportunities for employee autonomy in decision-making 

6 What's the best part about our work environment?
What aspect(s) make coming into this workplace enjoyable?

7. **Challenges ahead?**

8 How can we better support employee well-being and mental health in general:

a) By providing more wellness programs & resources
b) Through increased transparency regarding work-life balance expectations 
c) With regular check-ins from management/leadership

9. **What's the most important?**
When it comes to our company culture, what value or principle do you think is crucial for us (and why)?

10 What would make a significant positive impact on your job satisfaction?
Is there something we could implement that wouldn't require major changes?

Thank YOU! Your input will help shape initiatives and support the growth of everyone within this organization!

b) No

a) Yes
b) No

**Internal Mobility Opportunities Questionnaire**

As part of our ongoing efforts to support employee growth, we want to hear from you about your experiences and perspectives regarding internal job postings. Your input will help us better understand the needs and concerns related to career advancement within [Company Name]. Please take a few minutes to answer these questions honestly.

**Section 1: Awareness & Interest**

1.* How often do you check our company's intranet or HR portal for new job openings?

a) Daily
b) Weekly 
c) Monthly  
d) Rarely/Seldom

2. Are internal mobility opportunities something that interests and motivates you? 

Yes / No (please specify)

**Section 2: Barriers & Challenges**

3.* What do YOU think is the biggest obstacle to exploring or pursuing an open position within [Company Name]?

(Open-ended text field for respondents' written responses)
4. Have there been any instances where internal job postings were not clearly communicated, making it difficult for you (or others) to apply? 

Yes / No

**Section 3: Job Search & Application**

5.* How do YOU typically find out about new openings within [Company Name]?

a) Company intranet/HR portal
b) Manager or supervisor notification 
c) Networking with colleagues/friends  
d) Online job boards/social media

* Career advancement opportunities   
* Better work-life balance    
* New skills/challenges     
* Increased salary/benefits

**Section 4: Feedback & Suggestions**

7.* Have you ever applied or considered applying, but ultimately decided not pursue the opportunity?

Yes / No

9* Are there any specific training programs, mentorship initiatives, or professional development opportunities that could enhance your skills and prepare you better for future roles within [Company Name] ?

(Select all applicable)
a) Leadership/management courses
b) Technical skill-building workshops 
c) Soft-skills (communication/teamwork etc.)  
d) Industry-specific certifications   
e) Other: _______________________________________

**Section 5: Closing**

10.* Any additional comments or suggestions regarding internal mobility opportunities within [Company Name]?

(Open-ended text field for respondents' written responses)

1. **How would you rate overall satisfaction with your first week(s) at [Company Name]?**
a) Extremely Satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied, but some areas for improvement were noted.
c) Neutral - it was okay; nothing particularly stood out to me either way.
d) Disappointed/Somewhere in between

a) Clear instructions and guidelines
b) Engaging training sessions or workshops 
c) Accessible resources, such as documentation/manuals/intranet site)

a) Learning new software/hardware
b) Understanding company policies and procedures

d) Other [please specify]

b) Somewhat - it would be nice if we had some structured activities.

a.) Public acknowledgement

a) Daily/Monthly

Please share your thoughts, suggestions!

c)
Acknowledging my efforts and contributions

   a) Daily/Weekly (e.g., shout-outs, team meetings etc.)
    b) Monthly Quarterly or Semi-annually 
     c) Annually 

3.

a)
Public recognition at company-wide events
b)
Private acknowledgement from supervisor/team lead/manager

c)
Monetary rewards (bonuses, gift cards etc.)
d)
Other [please specify]

   a) Desire for personal growth & development 
    b) Sense of accomplishment/completion
     c) Recognition from peers or supervisors

a) Personalized message/video/letter etc.  
b) Public acknowledgement at company-wide events

c) Monetary rewards/bonuses/gift cards 
d) Other [please specify]

6.

8. How important are Recognition & Rewards in your decision-making process when considering a new job or career opportunity?
   Not Important Somewhat Unimportant Neutral Very Importance Extremely 

9.

a) Recognizing diverse contributions from various departments

b) Celebrating milestones & achievements across teams
c) Fostering a culture where everyone feels valued 
d) Other [please specify]

10. Are there any specific Recognition or Rewards programs you've experienced in previous roles/organizations?
   Yes No (If yes, please describe briefly)

11.
Any additional comments/suggestions on how we can improve recognition practices within your department/team?

Thank You for taking the time to share Your valuable insights!

Note that I've used the `1` type for questions `Q1`, `Q2`, `Q3`, and `Q5`, which corresponds to the "ID" type, and `2` type for question `Q2`, which corresponds to the "DESCRIPTION" type.

c) No/Not really

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire for investigating workplace environment:

**Workplace Environmental Survey**

We value our employees' opinions about their work experience, including factors that affect job satisfaction and overall well-being in the office setting. Your input will help us identify areas of strength as we strive to create an optimal workspace.

Please answer these questions honestly based on your experiences at [Company Name].

1.
How would you rate the physical comfort level (temperature, lighting) within our offices?

a) Very comfortable
b) Somewhat uncomfortable but manageable
c) Uncomfortable; needs improvement

2. What do we need to improve or add in terms of workspace amenities? Please share your thoughts on:

* Quiet areas for focused work?
* Collaborative spaces with whiteboards and breakout rooms?
* Accessible breakrooms, vending machines, etc.
3.

How would you rate the overall cleanliness level within our offices?

a) Excellent; always spotless
b) Good but could be better in some spots
c) Fair/poor

4. What do we need to improve or add regarding noise levels and distractions? Please share your thoughts on:

* Noise-cancelling headphones?
* Soundproofing materials for private areas?
5.

How would you rate the overall sense of community, camaraderie among colleagues?

a) Excellent; feels like a second family
b) Good but could be better with more team-building activities or social events

c) Fair/poor – we don't really interact outside work tasks
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions
